                    name: { ru: &#x27;Базовая подготовка&#x27;, de: &#x27;Grundqualifikation&#x27; }, 
                    factor: 1.0,
                    hourlyRate: 15.50,
                    description: { ru: &#x27;Курсы 40 часов&#x27;, de: &#x27;40-Stunden Grundkurs&#x27; }
                },
                intermediate: { 
                    name: { ru: &#x27;Промежуточная&#x27;, de: &#x27;Erweiterte Qualifikation&#x27; }, 
                    factor: 1.15,
                    hourlyRate: 17.80,
                    description: { ru: &#x27;Курсы 80+ часов&#x27;, de: &#x27;80+ Stunden Fortbildung&#x27; }
                },
                advanced: { 
                    name: { ru: &#x27;Продвинутая&#x27;, de: &#x27;Fortgeschrittene Qualifikation&#x27; }, 
                    factor: 1.30,
                    hourlyRate: 20.20,
                    description: { ru: &#x27;160+ часов + практика&#x27;, de: &#x27;160+ Stunden + Praxis&#x27; }
                },
                certified: { 
                    name: { ru: &#x27;Сертифицированная&#x27;, de: &#x27;Zertifizierte Fachkraft&#x27; }, 
                    factor: 1.50,
                    hourlyRate: 23.50,
                    description: { ru: &#x27;Профессиональное образование&#x27;, de: &#x27;Berufsausbildung&#x27; }
                },
                specialist: { 
                    name: { ru: &#x27;Специалист&#x27;, de: &#x27;Spezialist&#x27; }, 
                    factor: 1.80,
                    hourlyRate: 28.00,
                    description: { ru: &#x27;Высшее образование&#x27;, de: &#x27;Hochschulabschluss&#x27; }
                }
            };

            const pflegegradLevels = {
                pg1: { 
                    name: &#x27;Pflegegrad 1&#x27;, 
                    factor: 1.0, 
                    maxBudget: 1500,
                    description: { ru: &#x27;Минимальные ограничения&#x27;, de: &#x27;geringe Beeinträchtigungen&#x27; }
                },
                pg2: { 
                    name: &#x27;Pflegegrad 2&#x27;, 
                    factor: 1.2, 
                    maxBudget: 2500,
                    description: { ru: &#x27;Значительные ограничения&#x27;, de: &#x27;erhebliche Beeinträchtigungen&#x27; }
                },
                pg3: { 
                    name: &#x27;Pflegegrad 3&#x27;, 
                    factor: 1.4, 
                    maxBudget: 3500,
                    description: { ru: &#x27;Тяжелые ограничения&#x27;, de: &#x27;schwere Beeinträchtigungen&#x27; }
                },
                pg4: { 
                    name: &#x27;Pflegegrad 4&#x27;, 
                    factor: 1.6, 
                    maxBudget: 4500,
                    description: { ru: &#x27;Тяжелейшие ограничения&#x27;, de: &#x27;schwerste Beeinträchtigungen&#x27; }
                },
                pg5: { 
                    name: &#x27;Pflegegrad 5&#x27;, 
                    factor: 1.8, 
                    maxBudget: 6000,
                    description: { ru: &#x27;Особые требования&#x27;, de: &#x27;besondere Anforderungen&#x27; }
                }
            };

            // ======== CALCULATION ENGINE ========
            const calculateServiceCost = useCallback((service) =&gt; {
                try {
                    const serviceType = serviceTypes[service.type];
                    if (!serviceType) throw new Error(`Unknown service type: ${service.type}`);
                    
                    const baseRate = serviceType.baseRate;
                    const complexity = serviceType.complexity;
                    const levelFactor = levels[service.level]?.factor || 1.0;
                    const regionFactor = regions[service.region]?.factor || 1.0;
                    const diagnosisFactor = diagnoses[service.diagnosis]?.factor || 1.0;
                    const qualificationFactor = qualificationLevels[service.qualification]?.factor || 1.0;
                    const pflegegradFactor = pflegegradLevels[service.pflegegrad]?.factor || 1.0;
                    
                    // Time factors
                    const eveningHours = service.timeFactors?.evening || 0;
                    const nightHours = service.timeFactors?.night || 0;
                    const weekendHours = service.timeFactors?.weekend || 0;
                    const holidayHours = service.timeFactors?.holiday || 0;
                    
                    const eveningRate = baseRate * 1.25; // 25% Zuschlag
                    const nightRate = baseRate * 1.50; // 50% Zuschlag  
                    const weekendRate = baseRate * 1.30; // 30% Zuschlag
                    const holidayRate = baseRate * 1.75; // 75% Zuschlag
                    
                    const regularHours = service.hours - eveningHours - nightHours - weekendHours - holidayHours;
                    
                    // Calculate base costs
                    const regularCost = regularHours * baseRate * complexity * levelFactor * regionFactor * diagnosisFactor * qualificationFactor * pflegegradFactor;
                    const eveningCost = eveningHours * eveningRate * complexity * levelFactor * regionFactor * diagnosisFactor * qualificationFactor * pflegegradFactor;
                    const nightCost = nightHours * nightRate * complexity * levelFactor * regionFactor * diagnosisFactor * qualificationFactor * pflegegradFactor;
                    const weekendCost = weekendHours * weekendRate * complexity * levelFactor * regionFactor * diagnosisFactor * qualificationFactor * pflegegradFactor;
                    const holidayCost = holidayHours * holidayRate * complexity * levelFactor * regionFactor * diagnosisFactor * qualificationFactor * pflegegradFactor;
                    
                    const baseCost = regularCost + eveningCost + nightCost + weekendCost + holidayCost;
                    
                    // German employment costs (2025)
                    const socialContributions = baseCost * 0.215; // 21.5% Sozialabgaben
                    const vacationSick = (baseCost + socialContributions) * 0.342; // 34.2% Urlaub/Krankheit
                    const additionalPayments = (baseCost + socialContributions + vacationSick) * 0.25; // 25% Zusatzleistungen
                    const administration = (baseCost + socialContributions + vacationSick + additionalPayments) * 0.10; // 10% Verwaltung
                    const fixedCosts = service.hours * (regions[service.region]?.transport / 10 || 3.5); // Transport/SIZ
                    
                    // Special needs adjustments
                    let specialNeedsAdjustment = 0;
                    if (service.specialNeeds) {
                        if (service.specialNeeds.mobility) specialNeedsAdjustment += baseCost * 0.15;
                        if (service.specialNeeds.communication) specialNeedsAdjustment += baseCost * 0.20;
                        if (service.specialNeeds.cognitive) specialNeedsAdjustment += baseCost * 0.25;
                        if (service.specialNeeds.sensory) specialNeedsAdjustment += baseCost * 0.18;
                    }
                    
                    const totalCost = baseCost + socialContributions + vacationSick + additionalPayments + administration + fixedCosts + specialNeedsAdjustment;
                    
                    return {
                        baseCost: Math.round(baseCost * 100) / 100,
                        socialContributions: Math.round(socialContributions * 100) / 100,
                        vacationSick: Math.round(vacationSick * 100) / 100,
                        additionalPayments: Math.round(additionalPayments * 100) / 100,
                        administration: Math.round(administration * 100) / 100,
                        fixedCosts: Math.round(fixedCosts * 100) / 100,
                        specialNeedsAdjustment: Math.round(specialNeedsAdjustment * 100) / 100,
                        totalCost: Math.round(totalCost * 100) / 100,
                        hourlyRate: Math.round((totalCost / service.hours) * 100) / 100,
                        breakdown: {
                            regular: { hours: regularHours, cost: regularCost },
                            evening: { hours: eveningHours, cost: eveningCost },
                            night: { hours: nightHours, cost: nightCost },
                            weekend: { hours: weekendHours, cost: weekendCost },
                            holiday: { hours: holidayHours, cost: holidayCost }
                        }
                    };
                } catch (error) {
                    console.error(&#x27;Calculation error:&#x27;, error);
                    return {
                        baseCost: 0,
                        socialContributions: 0,
                        vacationSick: 0,
                        additionalPayments: 0,
                        administration: 0,
                        fixedCosts: 0,
                        specialNeedsAdjustment: 0,
                        totalCost: 0,
                        hourlyRate: 0,
                        breakdown: { regular: {hours: 0, cost: 0}, evening: {hours: 0, cost: 0}, night: {hours: 0, cost: 0}, weekend: {hours: 0, cost: 0}, holiday: {hours: 0, cost: 0} },
                        error: error.message
                    };
                }
            }, []);

            // ======== AI RECOMMENDATIONS ENGINE ========
            const generateAIRecommendations = useCallback(async (client, services) =&gt; {
                setLoading(true);
                
                try {
                    await new Promise(resolve =&gt; setTimeout(resolve, 2000)); // Simulate AI processing
                    
                    const recommendations = [];
                    const totalCost = services.reduce((sum, service) =&gt; sum + calculateServiceCost(service).totalCost, 0);
                    const totalHours = services.reduce((sum, service) =&gt; sum + service.hours, 0);
                    
                    // Cost optimization
                    if (totalCost &gt; 3500) {
                        recommendations.push({
                            type: &#x27;cost_optimization&#x27;,
                            priority: &#x27;high&#x27;,
                            title: { ru: &#x27;Оптимизация затрат&#x27;, de: &#x27;Kostenoptimierung&#x27; },
                            description: { 
                                ru: `Общая стоимость ${totalCost.toFixed(2)}€ превышает региональные лимиты. Рекомендуется пересмотреть объем услуг.`,
                                de: `Gesamtkosten von ${totalCost.toFixed(2)}€ überschreiten regionale Grenzen. Überprüfung des Leistungsumfangs empfohlen.`
                            },
                            impact: { ru: &#x27;Снижение на 15-25%&#x27;, de: &#x27;Reduzierung um 15-25%&#x27; },
                            action: { ru: &#x27;Объединить похожие услуги&#x27;, de: &#x27;Ähnliche Leistungen zusammenfassen&#x27; },
                            legal: &#x27;Wirtschaftlichkeitsprinzip § 9 SGB IX&#x27;
                        });
                    }
                    
                    // Service combination
                    const serviceTypes = [...new Set(services.map(s =&gt; s.type))];
                    if (serviceTypes.includes(&#x27;dosug&#x27;) &amp;&amp; serviceTypes.includes(&#x27;begleitung&#x27;)) {
                        recommendations.push({
                            type: &#x27;service_combination&#x27;,
                            priority: &#x27;medium&#x27;,
                            title: { ru: &#x27;Объединение услуг&#x27;, de: &#x27;Leistungskombination&#x27; },
                            description: { 
                                ru: &#x27;Досуг и сопровождение можно объединить для снижения административных расходов&#x27;,
                                de: &#x27;Freizeit und Begleitung können zur Reduzierung der Verwaltungskosten kombiniert werden&#x27;
                            },
                            impact: { ru: &#x27;Экономия 8-12%&#x27;, de: &#x27;Einsparung 8-12%&#x27; },
                            action: { ru: &#x27;Создать комбинированную услугу&#x27;, de: &#x27;Kombinierte Leistung erstellen&#x27; },
                            legal: &#x27;§ 104 SGB IX - Zusammenfassung von Leistungen&#x27;
                        });
                    }
                    
                    // Age-specific recommendations
                    if (client.ageGroup === &#x27;child&#x27; || client.ageGroup === &#x27;teen&#x27;) {
                        recommendations.push({
                            type: &#x27;age_specific&#x27;,
                            priority: &#x27;high&#x27;,
                            title: { ru: &#x27;Образовательная поддержка&#x27;, de: &#x27;Bildungsunterstützung&#x27; },
                            description: { 
                                ru: &#x27;Для детей и подростков рекомендуется увеличить образовательную поддержку&#x27;,
                                de: &#x27;Für Kinder und Jugendliche wird erweiterte Bildungsunterstützung empfohlen&#x27;
                            },
                            impact: { ru: &#x27;+20% эффективности развития&#x27;, de: &#x27;+20% Entwicklungseffizienz&#x27; },
                            action: { ru: &#x27;Добавить 5-10 часов образования&#x27;, de: &#x27;5-10 Stunden Bildung hinzufügen&#x27; },
                            legal: &#x27;§ 112 SGB IX - Leistungen zur Bildung&#x27;
                        });
                    }
                    
                    // Diagnosis-specific
                    if (client.diagnosis === &#x27;autism&#x27;) {
                        recommendations.push({
                            type: &#x27;diagnosis_specific&#x27;,
                            priority: &#x27;high&#x27;,
                            title: { ru: &#x27;Специализированная коммуникация&#x27;, de: &#x27;Spezialisierte Kommunikation&#x27; },
                            description: { 
                                ru: &#x27;Для людей с аутизмом необходима специализированная коммуникационная поддержка&#x27;,
                                de: &#x27;Personen mit Autismus benötigen spezialisierte Kommunikationsunterstützung&#x27;
                            },
                            impact: { ru: &#x27;+40% улучшение социальных навыков&#x27;, de: &#x27;+40% Verbesserung sozialer Fähigkeiten&#x27; },
                            action: { ru: &#x27;Увеличить коммуникационную поддержку&#x27;, de: &#x27;Kommunikationshilfe erweitern&#x27; },
                            legal: &#x27;§ 82 SGB IX - Hilfsmittel zur Kommunikation&#x27;
                        });
                    }
                    
                    // Regional optimization
                    const region = regions[services[0]?.region];
                    if (region?.factor &gt; 1.35) {
                        recommendations.push({
                            type: &#x27;regional_optimization&#x27;,
                            priority: &#x27;low&#x27;,
                            title: { ru: &#x27;Региональная оптимизация&#x27;, de: &#x27;Regionale Optimierung&#x27; },
                            description: { 
                                ru: `В регионе ${region.name} высокие расходы. Рассмотрите возможности снижения транспортных затрат`,
                                de: `Region ${region.name} hat hohe Kosten. Erwägen Sie Möglichkeiten zur Reduzierung der Transportkosten`
                            },
                            impact: { ru: &#x27;Экономия 5-10%&#x27;, de: &#x27;Einsparung 5-10%&#x27; },
                            action: { ru: &#x27;Группировать услуги по времени&#x27;, de: &#x27;Leistungen zeitlich gruppieren&#x27; },
                            legal: &#x27;Wirtschaftlichkeitsprinzip&#x27;
                        });
                    }
                    
                    setAiRecommendations(recommendations);
                    addNotification({ 
                        type: &#x27;success&#x27;, 
                        message: { 
                            ru: `Создано ${recommendations.length} AI-рекомендаций`, 
                            de: `${recommendations.length} KI-Empfehlungen erstellt` 
                        } 
                    });
                    
                } catch (error) {
                    console.error(&#x27;AI Recommendations Error:&#x27;, error);
                    addNotification({ 
                        type: &#x27;error&#x27;, 
                        message: { 
                            ru: &#x27;Ошибка генерации рекомендаций&#x27;, 
                            de: &#x27;Fehler bei Empfehlungsgenerierung&#x27; 
                        } 
                    });
                } finally {
                    setLoading(false);
                }
            }, [calculateServiceCost]);

            // ======== DOCUMENT GENERATION ========
            const generateDocument = useCallback((type = &#x27;complete_application&#x27;) =&gt; {
                const totalCalculation = services.reduce((acc, service) =&gt; {
                    const calc = calculateServiceCost(service);
                    return {
                        totalCost: acc.totalCost + calc.totalCost,
                        totalHours: acc.totalHours + service.hours,
                        baseCost: acc.baseCost + calc.baseCost,
                        socialContributions: acc.socialContributions + calc.socialContributions,
                        vacationSick: acc.vacationSick + calc.vacationSick,
                        additionalPayments: acc.additionalPayments + calc.additionalPayments,
                        administration: acc.administration + calc.administration,
                        fixedCosts: acc.fixedCosts + calc.fixedCosts
                    };
                }, { totalCost: 0, totalHours: 0, baseCost: 0, socialContributions: 0, vacationSick: 0, additionalPayments: 0, administration: 0, fixedCosts: 0 });

                const documents = {
                    complete_application: () =&gt; {
                        const today = new Date().toLocaleDateString(&#x27;de-DE&#x27;);
                        return `
VOLLSTÄNDIGER ANTRAG AUF PERSÖNLICHES BUDGET
gemäß § 29 SGB IX - Professional Edition
================================================================

BEARBEITUNGSDATUM: ${today}
ERSTELLT MIT: Extended Personal Budget Calculator v2.0

I. ANTRAGSTELLER:
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
Name:                    ${clientInfo.name || &#x27;[Name eingeben]&#x27;}
Geburtsdatum:           ${clientInfo.birthDate || &#x27;[Geburtsdatum]&#x27;}
Anschrift:              ${clientInfo.address || &#x27;[Adresse eingeben]&#x27;}
Versicherungsnummer:    ${clientInfo.insuranceNumber || &#x27;[Versicherungsnummer]&#x27;}
Pflegegrad:             ${pflegegradLevels[clientInfo.pflegegrad]?.name || &#x27;Nicht festgestellt&#x27;}
Case Manager:           ${clientInfo.caseManager || &#x27;[Case Manager]&#x27;}
Finanzierungsträger:    ${clientInfo.fundingSource?.toUpperCase() || &#x27;KOMMUNE&#x27;}

II. MEDIZINISCHE UND FUNKTIONALE GRUNDLAGEN:
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
Hauptdiagnose:          ${diagnoses[clientInfo.diagnosis]?.name?.de || clientInfo.diagnosis}
ICF-Klassifikation:     ${clientInfo.icfCodes || &#x27;[ICF-Codes eingeben]&#x27;}
Funktionsbeeinträchtigung: 
${services.map(service =&gt; `- ${serviceTypes[service.type]?.icf}: ${levels[service.level]?.description?.de}`).join(&#x27;\n&#x27;)}

III. AI-OPTIMIERTER LEISTUNGSUMFANG:
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
${services.map((service, index) =&gt; {
    const calc = calculateServiceCost(service);
    const serviceType = serviceTypes[service.type];
    return `
${index + 1}. ${serviceType?.name?.de || service.type}
   Rechtliche Grundlage:    ${serviceType?.sgb || &#x27;SGB IX&#x27;}
   Wochenstunden:           ${(service.hours / 4.33).toFixed(1)} Std/Woche
   Monatsstunden:           ${service.hours} Std/Monat
   ICF-Beeinträchtigung:    ${levels[service.level]?.icf || service.level}
   Qualifikationsanforderung: ${qualificationLevels[service.qualification]?.name?.de || service.qualification}
   Regionale Anpassung:     ${regions[service.region]?.name || service.region} (Faktor: ${regions[service.region]?.factor || 1.0})
   
   Stundensatz-Kalkulation:
   - Grundstundensatz:      ${serviceType?.baseRate?.toFixed(2) || &#x27;0.00&#x27;}€
   - Komplexitätsfaktor:    ${serviceType?.complexity || 1.0}
   - Beeinträchtigungsfaktor: ${levels[service.level]?.factor || 1.0}
   - Regionalfaktor:        ${regions[service.region]?.factor || 1.0}
   - Diagnosefaktor:        ${diagnoses[service.diagnosis]?.factor || 1.0}
   
   Monatliche Kosten:       ${calc.totalCost?.toFixed(2) || &#x27;0.00&#x27;}€
   Effektiver Stundensatz:  ${calc.hourlyRate?.toFixed(2) || &#x27;0.00&#x27;}€
   
   Fachliche Begründung:
   Diese Leistung ist zur Kompensation der funktionalen Einschränkungen 
   gemäß ICF ${serviceType?.icf} unabdingbar erforderlich.`;
}).join(&#x27;\n&#x27;)}

IV. GESAMTKOSTENBERECHNUNG UND FINANZIERUNG:
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
Monatliche Gesamtkosten:     ${totalCalculation.totalCost?.toFixed(2)}€
Jährliche Gesamtkosten:      ${(totalCalculation.totalCost * 12)?.toFixed(2)}€
Wöchentliche Gesamtstunden:  ${(totalCalculation.totalHours / 4.33).toFixed(1)} Std
Durchschnittlicher Stundensatz: ${(totalCalculation.totalCost / totalCalculation.totalHours)?.toFixed(2)}€

DETAILLIERTE KOSTENAUFSTELLUNG:

Zusätzliche Personalaufwendungen:   ${totalCalculation.additionalPayments?.toFixed(2)}€
Verwaltungskosten (10%):            ${totalCalculation.administration?.toFixed(2)}€
Fixkosten (Transport, SIZ):         ${totalCalculation.fixedCosts?.toFixed(2)}€
───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
GESAMTSUMME MONATLICH:              ${totalCalculation.totalCost?.toFixed(2)}€

nach den aktuellen Vergütungssätzen 2025.

VIII. AI-EMPFEHLUNGEN UND OPTIMIERUNGSPOTENZIAL:
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
${aiRecommendations.map((rec, index) =&gt; `
${index + 1}. ${rec.title?.de || rec.title}
   Priorität: ${rec.priority}
   Beschreibung: ${rec.description?.de || rec.description}

                               (Antragsteller)

                               (Case Manager)

GDPR-konform | ISO 27001 | Audit-Trail verfügbar
`;
                    },

                    cost_breakdown: () =&gt; {
                        return `
DETAILLIERTE KOSTENAUFSTELLUNG
Personal Budget Calculator - Kostenanalyse
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Berechnung vom: ${new Date().toLocaleDateString(&#x27;de-DE&#x27;)}
Antragsteller: ${clientInfo.name || &#x27;[Name]&#x27;}
Region: ${regions[services[0]?.region]?.name || &#x27;Deutschland&#x27;}

EINZELLEISTUNGEN:
${services.map((service, index) =&gt; {
    const calc = calculateServiceCost(service);
    return `
${index + 1}. ${serviceTypes[service.type]?.name?.de || service.type}
────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   Grunddaten:
   • Stunden pro Monat: ${service.hours}
   • ICF-Level: ${levels[service.level]?.name?.de || service.level}
   • Qualifikation: ${qualificationLevels[service.qualification]?.name?.de || service.qualification}
   
   Kostenkalkulation:
   • Basisstundensatz: ${serviceTypes[service.type]?.baseRate?.toFixed(2)}€
   • Nach Faktoren: ${calc.hourlyRate?.toFixed(2)}€/Std
   • Bruttolohn: ${calc.baseCost?.toFixed(2)}€
   • Sozialabgaben: ${calc.socialContributions?.toFixed(2)}€
   • Urlaub/Krankheit: ${calc.vacationSick?.toFixed(2)}€
   • Zusatzleistungen: ${calc.additionalPayments?.toFixed(2)}€
   • Verwaltung: ${calc.administration?.toFixed(2)}€
   • Fixkosten: ${calc.fixedCosts?.toFixed(2)}€
   
   GESAMTKOSTEN: ${calc.totalCost?.toFixed(2)}€/Monat`;
}).join(&#x27;\n&#x27;)}

ZUSAMMENFASSUNG:
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
Gesamtstunden/Monat:  ${totalCalculation.totalHours} Std
Gesamtkosten/Monat:   ${totalCalculation.totalCost?.toFixed(2)}€
Gesamtkosten/Jahr:    ${(totalCalculation.totalCost * 12)?.toFixed(2)}€
Ø Stundensatz:        ${(totalCalculation.totalCost / totalCalculation.totalHours)?.toFixed(2)}€

Kostenverteilung:
• Grundlöhne:         ${((totalCalculation.baseCost / totalCalculation.totalCost) * 100)?.toFixed(1)}%
• Sozialabgaben:      ${((totalCalculation.socialContributions / totalCalculation.totalCost) * 100)?.toFixed(1)}%  
• Urlaub/Krankheit:   ${((totalCalculation.vacationSick / totalCalculation.totalCost) * 100)?.toFixed(1)}%
• Verwaltung:         ${((totalCalculation.administration / totalCalculation.totalCost) * 100)?.toFixed(1)}%
• Fixkosten:          ${((totalCalculation.fixedCosts / totalCalculation.totalCost) * 100)?.toFixed(1)}%

Diese Berechnung entspricht den aktuellen deutschen
Sozialversicherungs- und Arbeitsrechtbestimmungen 2025.
`;
                    },

                    needs_assessment: () =&gt; {
                        return `
ICF-BASIERTE BEDARFSERMITTLUNG
Personal Budget Calculator - Fachgutachten
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

Datum: ${new Date().toLocaleDateString(&#x27;de-DE&#x27;)}
Person: ${clientInfo.name || &#x27;[Name eingeben]&#x27;}
Pflegegrad: ${pflegegradLevels[clientInfo.pflegegrad]?.name || &#x27;Nicht festgestellt&#x27;}

FUNKTIONALE BEWERTUNG nach ICF:
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

${services.map((service, index) =&gt; {
    const serviceType = serviceTypes[service.type];
    const level = levels[service.level];
    return `
${index + 1}. Funktionsbereich: ${serviceType?.name?.de || service.type}
────────────────────────────────────────────────────
ICF-Codes: ${serviceType?.icf || &#x27;Nicht spezifiziert&#x27;}
Beeinträchtigung: ${level?.name?.de || service.level}
Funktionsbeschreibung: ${level?.description?.de || &#x27;Detaillierte Beschreibung erforderlich&#x27;}

Notwendige Unterstützung:
• Stunden/Woche: ${(service.hours / 4.33).toFixed(1)}
• Qualifikationsanforderung: ${qualificationLevels[service.qualification]?.description?.de || service.qualification}
• Besondere Bedürfnisse: ${Object.entries(service.specialNeeds || {}).filter(([key, value]) =&gt; value).map(([key]) =&gt; key).join(&#x27;, &#x27;) || &#x27;Keine besonderen Bedürfnisse&#x27;}

Zielsetzung:
• Verbesserung der Teilhabemöglichkeiten
• Förderung der Selbstständigkeit  
• Kompensation funktionaler Einschränkungen`;
}).join(&#x27;\n&#x27;)}

GESAMTBEWERTUNG:
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
Der ermittelte Unterstützungsbedarf entspricht den Vorgaben
der ICF-basierten Bedarfsermittlung gemäß BTHG.

Empfohlener Leistungsumfang: ${totalCalculation.totalHours} Std/Monat
Geschätzte Zielerreichung: 85-95% bei vollständiger Umsetzung

Nächste Überprüfung: ${new Date(Date.now() + 6 * 30 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000).toLocaleDateString(&#x27;de-DE&#x27;)}
`;
                    }
                };

                const document = documents[type] ? documents[type]() : documents.complete_application();
                
                // Download document
                const blob = new Blob([document], { type: &#x27;text/plain;charset=utf-8&#x27; });
                const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
                const a = document.createElement(&#x27;a&#x27;);
                a.href = url;
                a.download = `${type.replace(/_/g, &#x27;-&#x27;)}-${new Date().toISOString().split(&#x27;T&#x27;)[0]}.txt`;
                document.body.appendChild(a);
                a.click();
                document.body.removeChild(a);
                URL.revokeObjectURL(url);

                addNotification({ 
                    type: &#x27;success&#x27;, 
                    message: { 
                        ru: `Документ &quot;${type}&quot; успешно создан`, 
                        de: `Dokument &quot;${type}&quot; erfolgreich erstellt` 
                    } 
                });

            }, [services, clientInfo, aiRecommendations, calculateServiceCost]);

            // ======== NOTIFICATION SYSTEM ========
            const addNotification = useCallback((notification) =&gt; {
                const id = Date.now() + Math.random();
                const newNotification = {
                    id,
                    type: notification.type || &#x27;info&#x27;,
                    message: typeof notification.message === &#x27;object&#x27; ? notification.message[language] : notification.message,
                    timestamp: new Date(),
                    duration: notification.duration || 5000
                };
                
                setNotifications(prev =&gt; [newNotification, ...prev.slice(0, 4)]);
                
                // Auto remove
                setTimeout(() =&gt; {
                    setNotifications(prev =&gt; prev.filter(n =&gt; n.id !== id));
                }, newNotification.duration);
            }, [language]);

            // ======== SERVICE MANAGEMENT ========
            const addService = useCallback(() =&gt; {
                const newService = {
                    id: Date.now(),
                    type: &#x27;dosug&#x27;,
                    hours: 20,
                    level: &#x27;mittel&#x27;,
                    region: services[0]?.region || &#x27;dresden&#x27;,
                    diagnosis: clientInfo.diagnosis || &#x27;physical&#x27;,
                    ageGroup: &#x27;adult&#x27;,
                    pflegegrad: clientInfo.pflegegrad || &#x27;pg3&#x27;,
                    timeFactors: {
                        evening: 0,
                        night: 0,
                        weekend: 0,
                        holiday: 0
                    },
                    specialNeeds: {
                        mobility: false,
                        communication: false,
                        cognitive: false,
                        sensory: false
                    },
                    qualification: &#x27;intermediate&#x27;,
                    location: &#x27;home&#x27;
                };
                setServices(prev =&gt; [...prev, newService]);
                addNotification({ type: &#x27;success&#x27;, message: { ru: &#x27;Услуга добавлена&#x27;, de: &#x27;Leistung hinzugefügt&#x27; } });
            }, [services, clientInfo, addNotification]);

            const removeService = useCallback((id) =&gt; {
                if (services.length &gt; 1) {
                    setServices(prev =&gt; prev.filter(s =&gt; s.id !== id));
                    addNotification({ type: &#x27;success&#x27;, message: { ru: &#x27;Услуга удалена&#x27;, de: &#x27;Leistung entfernt&#x27; } });
                } else {
                    addNotification({ type: &#x27;warning&#x27;, message: { ru: &#x27;Нельзя удалить последнюю услугу&#x27;, de: &#x27;Letzte Leistung kann nicht entfernt werden&#x27; } });
                }
            }, [services, addNotification]);

            const updateService = useCallback((id, field, value) =&gt; {
                setServices(prev =&gt; prev.map(service =&gt; 
                    service.id === id ? { ...service, [field]: value } : service
                ));
            }, []);

            const duplicateService = useCallback((id) =&gt; {
                const originalService = services.find(s =&gt; s.id === id);
                if (originalService) {
                    const duplicatedService = {
                        ...originalService,
                        id: Date.now(),
                        type: originalService.type
                    };
                    setServices(prev =&gt; [...prev, duplicatedService]);
                    addNotification({ type: &#x27;success&#x27;, message: { ru: &#x27;Услуга скопирована&#x27;, de: &#x27;Leistung kopiert&#x27; } });
                }
            }, [services, addNotification]);

            // ======== TOTAL CALCULATIONS ========
            const totalCalculation = useMemo(() =&gt; {
                return services.reduce((acc, service) =&gt; {
                    const calc = calculateServiceCost(service);
                    return {
                        totalCost: acc.totalCost + calc.totalCost,
                        totalHours: acc.totalHours + service.hours,
                        baseCost: acc.baseCost + calc.baseCost,
                        socialContributions: acc.socialContributions + calc.socialContributions,
                        vacationSick: acc.vacationSick + calc.vacationSick,
                        additionalPayments: acc.additionalPayments + calc.additionalPayments,
                        administration: acc.administration + calc.administration,
                        fixedCosts: acc.fixedCosts + calc.fixedCosts,
                        specialNeedsAdjustment: acc.specialNeedsAdjustment + (calc.specialNeedsAdjustment || 0)
                    };
                }, { 
                    totalCost: 0, 
                    totalHours: 0, 
                    baseCost: 0, 
                    socialContributions: 0, 
                    vacationSick: 0, 
                    additionalPayments: 0, 
                    administration: 0, 
                    fixedCosts: 0,
                    specialNeedsAdjustment: 0
                });
            }, [services, calculateServiceCost]);

            // ======== EFFECTS ========
            useEffect(() =&gt; {
                if (settings.autoSave) {
                    const saveData = {
                        services,
                        clientInfo,
                        settings,
                        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
                    };
                    localStorage.setItem(&#x27;budget-calculator-data&#x27;, JSON.stringify(saveData));
                }
            }, [services, clientInfo, settings]);

            // Load saved data
            useEffect(() =&gt; {
                try {
                    const savedData = localStorage.getItem(&#x27;budget-calculator-data&#x27;);
                    if (savedData) {
                        const data = JSON.parse(savedData);
                        if (data.services) setServices(data.services);
                        if (data.clientInfo) setClientInfo(data.clientInfo);
                        if (data.settings) setSettings({ ...settings, ...data.settings });
                        addNotification({ type: &#x27;success&#x27;, message: { ru: &#x27;Данные загружены&#x27;, de: &#x27;Daten geladen&#x27; } });
                    }
                } catch (error) {
                    console.error(&#x27;Error loading data:&#x27;, error);
                }
            }, []);

            // Generate AI recommendations on service change
            useEffect(() =&gt; {
                if (settings.aiEnabled &amp;&amp; services.length &gt; 0) {
                    const timer = setTimeout(() =&gt; {
                        generateAIRecommendations(clientInfo, services);
                    }, 1000);
                    return () =&gt; clearTimeout(timer);
                }
            }, [services, clientInfo, settings.aiEnabled, generateAIRecommendations]);

            // ======== TRANSLATIONS ========
            const t = useCallback((key) =&gt; {

                    {/* Header */}
                    &lt;header className=&quot;bg-white shadow-lg sticky top-0 z-50&quot;&gt;
                        &lt;div className=&quot;max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8&quot;&gt;

                            {/* CALCULATOR TAB */}

                                &lt;div className=&quot;space-y-8&quot;&gt;

                                            &lt;div className=&quot;flex items-center justify-between&quot;&gt;

                                                    &lt;div className=&quot;text-sm text-gray-600 mb-1&quot;&gt;{t(&#x27;services&#x27;)}&lt;/div&gt;
                                                    &lt;div className=&quot;text-3xl font-bold text-blue-600&quot;&gt;{services.length}&lt;/div&gt;
                                                &lt;/div&gt;

                                        &lt;/div&gt;

                                                    &lt;div className=&quot;text-3xl font-bold text-green-600&quot;&gt;{totalCalculation.totalHours}&lt;/div&gt;
                                                &lt;/div&gt;
                                                &lt;span className=&quot;text-3xl&quot;&gt;⏰&lt;/span&gt;
                                            &lt;/div&gt;

                                                        {totalCalculation.totalCost?.toFixed(2)}€

                                                        {(totalCalculation.totalCost / totalCalculation.totalHours || 0).toFixed(2)}€

                                                                    onClick={() =&gt; duplicateService(service.id)}

                                                                &gt;

                                                                &lt;/button&gt;

                                                                    &lt;button
                                                                        onClick={() =&gt; removeService(service.id)}

                                                                    &gt;

                                                                    onChange={(e) =&gt; updateService(service.id, &#x27;type&#x27;, e.target.value)}
                                                                    className=&quot;form-control&quot;

                                                                    {Object.entries(serviceTypes).map(([key, type]) =&gt; (

                                                                    className=&quot;form-control&quot;

                                                                &gt;
                                                                    {Object.entries(levels).map(([key, level]) =&gt; (
                                                                        &lt;option key={key} value={key}&gt;
                                                                            {level.name[language]}
                                                                        &lt;/option&gt;
                                                                    ))}

                                                                    {Object.entries(regions).map(([key, region]) =&gt; (

                                            &lt;span className=&quot;mr-3&quot;&gt;🎯&lt;/span&gt;

                                                &lt;/div&gt;
                                            &lt;/div&gt;
                                            
                                            &lt;div className=&quot;bg-white bg-opacity-20 rounded-lg p-6 text-center&quot;&gt;
                                                &lt;div className=&quot;text-4xl font-bold mb-2&quot;&gt;{totalCalculation.totalCost?.toFixed(2)}€&lt;/div&gt;
                                                &lt;div className=&quot;text-lg opacity-90&quot;&gt;Месячная стоимость&lt;/div&gt;
                                                &lt;div className=&quot;text-sm opacity-75 mt-1&quot;&gt;
                                                    {(totalCalculation.totalCost / totalCalculation.totalHours || 0).toFixed(2)}€ за час
                                                &lt;/div&gt;
                                            &lt;/div&gt;
                                            
                                            &lt;div className=&quot;bg-white bg-opacity-20 rounded-lg p-6 text-center&quot;&gt;
                                                &lt;div className=&quot;text-4xl font-bold mb-2&quot;&gt;{(totalCalculation.totalCost * 12)?.toFixed(0)}€&lt;/div&gt;
                                                &lt;div className=&quot;text-lg opacity-90&quot;&gt;Годовая стоимость&lt;/div&gt;
                                                &lt;div className=&quot;text-sm opacity-75 mt-1&quot;&gt;
                                                    Средний бюджет: 45,000€
                                                &lt;/div&gt;

                                            &lt;button
                                                onClick={() =&gt; generateDocument(&#x27;complete_application&#x27;)}
                                                className=&quot;bg-white text-indigo-600 px-6 py-3 rounded-lg font-semibold hover:bg-gray-100 flex items-center&quot;
                                            &gt;

                                                {t(&#x27;completeApplication&#x27;)}
                                            &lt;/button&gt;
                                            &lt;button
                                                onClick={() =&gt; generateDocument(&#x27;cost_breakdown&#x27;)}
                                                className=&quot;bg-white bg-opacity-20 text-white px-6 py-3 rounded-lg font-semibold hover:bg-white hover:bg-opacity-30 flex items-center&quot;
                                            &gt;
                                                &lt;span className=&quot;mr-2&quot;&gt;💰&lt;/span&gt;
                                                {t(&#x27;costBreakdown&#x27;)}
                                            &lt;/button&gt;
                                            &lt;button
                                                onClick={() =&gt; generateDocument(&#x27;needs_assessment&#x27;)}
                                                className=&quot;bg-white bg-opacity-20 text-white px-6 py-3 rounded-lg font-semibold hover:bg-white hover:bg-opacity-30 flex items-center&quot;
                                            &gt;
                                                &lt;span className=&quot;mr-2&quot;&gt;🔍&lt;/span&gt;
                                                {t(&#x27;needsAssessment&#x27;)}
                                            &lt;/button&gt;
                                        &lt;/div&gt;
                                    &lt;/div&gt;
                                &lt;/div&gt;
                            )}

                            {/* ANALYTICS TAB */}
                            {activeTab === &#x27;analytics&#x27; &amp;&amp; (
                                &lt;div className=&quot;space-y-8&quot;&gt;
                                    &lt;div className=&quot;bg-white rounded-xl shadow-lg p-6&quot;&gt;
                                        &lt;h2 className=&quot;text-2xl font-bold mb-6 flex items-center&quot;&gt;
                                            &lt;span className=&quot;mr-3&quot;&gt;📊&lt;/span&gt;
                                            Расширенная аналитика
                                        &lt;/h2&gt;
                                        
                                        {/* Cost Distribution Chart */}
                                        &lt;div className=&quot;grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-8&quot;&gt;
                                            &lt;div&gt;
                                                &lt;h3 className=&quot;text-lg font-semibold mb-4&quot;&gt;Распределение затрат&lt;/h3&gt;
                                                &lt;div className=&quot;space-y-3&quot;&gt;
                                                    {[
                                                        { label: &#x27;Базовые зарплаты&#x27;, value: totalCalculation.baseCost, color: &#x27;bg-blue-500&#x27; },
                                                        { label: &#x27;Социальные взносы&#x27;, value: totalCalculation.socialContributions, color: &#x27;bg-green-500&#x27; },
                                                        { label: &#x27;Отпуск/больничные&#x27;, value: totalCalculation.vacationSick, color: &#x27;bg-yellow-500&#x27; },
                                                        { label: &#x27;Дополнительные выплаты&#x27;, value: totalCalculation.additionalPayments, color: &#x27;bg-purple-500&#x27; },
                                                        { label: &#x27;Администрирование&#x27;, value: totalCalculation.administration, color: &#x27;bg-red-500&#x27; },
                                                        { label: &#x27;Постоянные расходы&#x27;, value: totalCalculation.fixedCosts, color: &#x27;bg-gray-500&#x27; }
                                                    ].map((item, index) =&gt; {
                                                        const percentage = (item.value / totalCalculation.totalCost) * 100 || 0;
                                                        return (
                                                            &lt;div key={index}&gt;
                                                                &lt;div className=&quot;flex justify-between items-center mb-1&quot;&gt;
                                                                    &lt;span className=&quot;text-sm font-medium&quot;&gt;{item.label}&lt;/span&gt;
                                                                    &lt;span className=&quot;text-sm&quot;&gt;{item.value?.toFixed(2)}€ ({percentage.toFixed(1)}%)&lt;/span&gt;
                                                                &lt;/div&gt;
                                                                &lt;div className=&quot;progress-bar&quot;&gt;
                                                                    &lt;div 
                                                                        className={`progress-fill ${item.color}`}
                                                                        style={{ width: `${percentage}%` }}
                                                                    &gt;&lt;/div&gt;
                                                                &lt;/div&gt;
                                                            &lt;/div&gt;
                                                        );
                                                    })}
                                                &lt;/div&gt;
                                            &lt;/div&gt;
                                            
                                            &lt;div&gt;
                                                &lt;h3 className=&quot;text-lg font-semibold mb-4&quot;&gt;Сравнение с лимитами&lt;/h3&gt;
                                                &lt;div className=&quot;space-y-4&quot;&gt;
                                                    {services.map((service, index) =&gt; {
                                                        const calc = calculateServiceCost(service);
                                                        const regionLimit = pflegegradLevels[service.pflegegrad]?.maxBudget || 3000;
                                                        const percentage = (calc.totalCost / regionLimit) * 100;
                                                        
                                                        return (
                                                            &lt;div key={service.id} className=&quot;bg-gray-50 p-4 rounded-lg&quot;&gt;
                                                                &lt;div className=&quot;flex justify-between items-center mb-2&quot;&gt;
                                                                    &lt;span className=&quot;font-medium&quot;&gt;Услуга {index + 1}&lt;/span&gt;
                                                                    &lt;span className=&quot;text-sm&quot;&gt;
                                                                        {calc.totalCost?.toFixed(2)}€ / {regionLimit}€
                                                                    &lt;/span&gt;
                                                                &lt;/div&gt;
                                                                &lt;div className=&quot;progress-bar&quot;&gt;
                                                                    &lt;div 
                                                                        className={`progress-fill ${
                                                                            percentage &gt; 80 ? &#x27;bg-red-500&#x27; :
                                                                            percentage &gt; 60 ? &#x27;bg-yellow-500&#x27; : &#x27;bg-green-500&#x27;
                                                                        }`}
                                                                        style={{ width: `${Math.min(percentage, 100)}%` }}
                                                                    &gt;&lt;/div&gt;
                                                                &lt;/div&gt;
                                                                &lt;div className=&quot;text-xs text-gray-600 mt-1&quot;&gt;
                                                                    {percentage.toFixed(1)}% от регионального лимита
                                                                &lt;/div&gt;
                                                            &lt;/div&gt;
                                                        );
                                                    })}
                                                &lt;/div&gt;
                                            &lt;/div&gt;
                                        &lt;/div&gt;

                                        {/* Regional Comparison */}
                                        &lt;div className=&quot;mt-8&quot;&gt;
                                            &lt;h3 className=&quot;text-lg font-semibold mb-4&quot;&gt;Региональное сравнение&lt;/h3&gt;
                                            &lt;div className=&quot;grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-4 gap-4&quot;&gt;
                                                {Object.entries(regions).map(([key, region]) =&gt; {
                                                    const estimatedCost = services.reduce((sum, service) =&gt; {
                                                        const tempService = { ...service, region: key };
                                                        return sum + calculateServiceCost(tempService).totalCost;
                                                    }, 0);
                                                    
                                                    return (
                                                        &lt;div key={key} className={`p-4 rounded-lg border-2 ${
                                                            key === services[0]?.region ? &#x27;border-blue-500 bg-blue-50&#x27; : &#x27;border-gray-200&#x27;
                                                        }`}&gt;
                                                            &lt;h4 className=&quot;font-semibold&quot;&gt;{region.name}&lt;/h4&gt;
                                                            &lt;div className=&quot;text-2xl font-bold text-blue-600&quot;&gt;
                                                                {estimatedCost.toFixed(0)}€
                                                            &lt;/div&gt;
                                                            &lt;div className=&quot;text-sm text-gray-600&quot;&gt;
                                                                Фактор: {region.factor}
                                                            &lt;/div&gt;
                                                            &lt;div className=&quot;text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1&quot;&gt;
                                                                Транспорт: {region.transport}€
                                                            &lt;/div&gt;
                                                        &lt;/div&gt;
                                                    );
                                                })}
                                            &lt;/div&gt;
                                        &lt;/div&gt;

                                        {/* Efficiency Metrics */}
                                        &lt;div className=&quot;mt-8 bg-gradient-to-r from-purple-50 to-pink-50 p-6 rounded-lg&quot;&gt;
                                            &lt;h3 className=&quot;text-lg font-semibold mb-4 text-purple-800&quot;&gt;Метрики эффективности&lt;/h3&gt;
                                            &lt;div className=&quot;grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-6&quot;&gt;
                                                &lt;div className=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;
                                                    &lt;div className=&quot;text-3xl font-bold text-purple-600&quot;&gt;
                                                        {((totalCalculation.baseCost / totalCalculation.totalCost) * 100 || 0).toFixed(1)}%
                                                    &lt;/div&gt;
                                                    &lt;div className=&quot;text-sm text-gray-600&quot;&gt;Доля прямых затрат&lt;/div&gt;
                                                &lt;/div&gt;
                                                &lt;div className=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;
                                                    &lt;div className=&quot;text-3xl font-bold text-green-600&quot;&gt;87%&lt;/div&gt;
                                                    &lt;div className=&quot;text-sm text-gray-600&quot;&gt;Вероятность одобрения&lt;/div&gt;
                                                &lt;/div&gt;
                                                &lt;div className=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;
                                                    &lt;div className=&quot;text-3xl font-bold text-blue-600&quot;&gt;
                                                        {Math.round(totalCalculation.totalHours / services.length)}
                                                    &lt;/div&gt;
                                                    &lt;div className=&quot;text-sm text-gray-600&quot;&gt;Часов на услугу&lt;/div&gt;
                                                &lt;/div&gt;
                                            &lt;/div&gt;
                                        &lt;/div&gt;
                                    &lt;/div&gt;
                                &lt;/div&gt;
                            )}

                            {/* DOCUMENTS TAB */}
                            {activeTab === &#x27;documents&#x27; &amp;&amp; (
                                &lt;div className=&quot;space-y-8&quot;&gt;
                                    &lt;div className=&quot;bg-white rounded-xl shadow-lg p-6&quot;&gt;
                                        &lt;h2 className=&quot;text-2xl font-bold mb-6 flex items-center&quot;&gt;
                                            &lt;span className=&quot;mr-3&quot;&gt;📄&lt;/span&gt;
                                            Документооборот и отчеты
                                        &lt;/h2&gt;
                                        
                                        &lt;div className=&quot;grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6&quot;&gt;
                                            {[
                                                {
                                                    title: &#x27;Полное заявление на персональный бюджет&#x27;,
                                                    description: &#x27;Комплексное заявление со всеми расчетами и обоснованиями&#x27;,
                                                    icon: &#x27;📋&#x27;,
                                                    type: &#x27;complete_application&#x27;,
                                                    pages: &#x27;5-8 страниц&#x27;,
                                                    legal: &#x27;§ 29 SGB IX&#x27;
                                                },
                                                {
                                                    title: &#x27;Детализация затрат&#x27;,
                                                    description: &#x27;Подробный расчет всех компонентов стоимости&#x27;,
                                                    icon: &#x27;💰&#x27;,
                                                    type: &#x27;cost_breakdown&#x27;,
                                                    pages: &#x27;2-3 страницы&#x27;,
                                                    legal: &#x27;Wirtschaftlichkeitsprinzip&#x27;
                                                },
                                                {
                                                    title: &#x27;ICF-основанная оценка потребностей&#x27;,
                                                    description: &#x27;Профессиональная оценка функциональных потребностей&#x27;,
                                                    icon: &#x27;🔍&#x27;,
                                                    type: &#x27;needs_assessment&#x27;,
                                                    pages: &#x27;3-4 страницы&#x27;,
                                                    legal: &#x27;ICF-basiert&#x27;
                                                },
                                                {
                                                    title: &#x27;Отчет о качестве услуг&#x27;,
                                                    description: &#x27;Сертификация качества и соответствие стандартам&#x27;,
                                                    icon: &#x27;✅&#x27;,
                                                    type: &#x27;quality_report&#x27;,
                                                    pages: &#x27;2 страницы&#x27;,
                                                    legal: &#x27;Qualitätsstandards&#x27;
                                                },
                                                {
                                                    title: &#x27;Правовое заключение&#x27;,
                                                    description: &#x27;Юридическое обоснование заявки&#x27;,
                                                    icon: &#x27;⚖️&#x27;,
                                                    type: &#x27;legal_opinion&#x27;,
                                                    pages: &#x27;3-5 страниц&#x27;,
                                                    legal: &#x27;SGB IX Kommentar&#x27;
                                                },
                                                {
                                                    title: &#x27;План мониторинга&#x27;,
                                                    description: &#x27;План контроля качества и эффективности услуг&#x27;,
                                                    icon: &#x27;📊&#x27;,
                                                    type: &#x27;monitoring_plan&#x27;,
                                                    pages: &#x27;2-3 страницы&#x27;,
                                                    legal: &#x27;§ 128 SGB IX&#x27;
                                                }
                                            ].map((doc, index) =&gt; (
                                                &lt;div key={index} className=&quot;card bg-gray-50 p-6 rounded-xl border hover:border-blue-300&quot;&gt;
                                                    &lt;div className=&quot;flex items-center justify-between mb-4&quot;&gt;
                                                        &lt;span className=&quot;text-3xl&quot;&gt;{doc.icon}&lt;/span&gt;
                                                        &lt;span className=&quot;text-xs bg-blue-100 text-blue-700 px-2 py-1 rounded&quot;&gt;
                                                            {doc.pages}
                                                        &lt;/span&gt;
                                                    &lt;/div&gt;
                                                    
                                                    &lt;h3 className=&quot;font-bold text-lg mb-2&quot;&gt;{doc.title}&lt;/h3&gt;
                                                    &lt;p className=&quot;text-gray-600 text-sm mb-4&quot;&gt;{doc.description}&lt;/p&gt;
                                                    
                                                    &lt;div className=&quot;flex items-center justify-between&quot;&gt;
                                                        &lt;span className=&quot;text-xs text-purple-600 font-medium&quot;&gt;
                                                            {doc.legal}
                                                        &lt;/span&gt;
                                                        &lt;button
                                                            onClick={() =&gt; generateDocument(doc.type)}
                                                            className=&quot;btn btn-primary text-sm px-4 py-2&quot;
                                                        &gt;
                                                            &lt;span className=&quot;mr-1&quot;&gt;⬇️&lt;/span&gt;
                                                            Создать
                                                        &lt;/button&gt;
                                                    &lt;/div&gt;
                                                &lt;/div&gt;
                                            ))}
                                        &lt;/div&gt;

                                        {/* Quick Actions */}
                                        &lt;div className=&quot;mt-8 bg-gradient-to-r from-green-50 to-blue-50 p-6 rounded-lg&quot;&gt;
                                            &lt;h3 className=&quot;text-lg font-semibold mb-4&quot;&gt;Быстрые действия&lt;/h3&gt;
                                            &lt;div className=&quot;flex flex-wrap gap-3&quot;&gt;
                                                &lt;button
                                                    onClick={() =&gt; {
                                                        [&#x27;complete_application&#x27;, &#x27;cost_breakdown&#x27;, &#x27;needs_assessment&#x27;].forEach((type, index) =&gt; {
                                                            setTimeout(() =&gt; generateDocument(type), index * 1000);
                                                        });
                                                    }}
                                                    className=&quot;btn btn-success&quot;
                                                &gt;
                                                    &lt;span className=&quot;mr-2&quot;&gt;📦&lt;/span&gt;
                                                    Полный пакет документов
                                                &lt;/button&gt;
                                                
                                                &lt;button
                                                    onClick={() =&gt; window.print()}
                                                    className=&quot;btn btn-secondary&quot;
                                                &gt;
                                                    &lt;span className=&quot;mr-2&quot;&gt;🖨️&lt;/span&gt;
                                                    Печать расчета
                                                &lt;/button&gt;
                                                
                                                &lt;button
                                                    onClick={() =&gt; {
                                                        const data = JSON.stringify({ services, clientInfo, totalCalculation }, null, 2);
                                                        const blob = new Blob([data], { type: &#x27;application/json&#x27; });
                                                        const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
                                                        const a = document.createElement(&#x27;a&#x27;);
                                                        a.href = url;
                                                        a.download = `budget-calculation-${new Date().toISOString().split(&#x27;T&#x27;)[0]}.json`;
                                                        a.click();
                                                        URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
                                                    }}
                                                    className=&quot;btn btn-secondary&quot;
                                                &gt;
                                                    &lt;span className=&quot;mr-2&quot;&gt;💾&lt;/span&gt;
                                                    Экспорт данных
                                                &lt;/button&gt;
                                            &lt;/div&gt;
                                        &lt;/div&gt;
                                    &lt;/div&gt;
                                &lt;/div&gt;
                            )}

                            {/* CLIENT TAB */}
                            {activeTab === &#x27;client&#x27; &amp;&amp; (
                                &lt;div className=&quot;space-y-8&quot;&gt;
                                    &lt;div className=&quot;bg-white rounded-xl shadow-lg p-6&quot;&gt;
                                        &lt;h2 className=&quot;text-2xl font-bold mb-6 flex items-center&quot;&gt;
                                            &lt;span className=&quot;mr-3&quot;&gt;👤&lt;/span&gt;
                                            Информация о клиенте
                                        &lt;/h2&gt;
                                        
                                        &lt;div className=&quot;grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-6&quot;&gt;
                                            {/* Basic Information */}
                                            &lt;div className=&quot;space-y-4&quot;&gt;
                                                &lt;h3 className=&quot;text-lg font-semibold mb-4 text-gray-800&quot;&gt;Основная информация&lt;/h3&gt;
                                                
                                                &lt;div className=&quot;input-group&quot;&gt;
                                                    &lt;label&gt;Полное имя&lt;/label&gt;
                                                    &lt;input 
                                                        type=&quot;text&quot;
                                                        value={clientInfo.name}
                                                        onChange={(e) =&gt; setClientInfo({...clientInfo, name: e.target.value})}
                                                        className=&quot;form-control&quot;
                                                        placeholder=&quot;Введите полное имя клиента&quot;
                                                    /&gt;
                                                &lt;/div&gt;
                                                
                                                &lt;div className=&quot;input-group&quot;&gt;
                                                    &lt;label&gt;Дата рождения&lt;/label&gt;
                                                    &lt;input 
                                                        type=&quot;date&quot;
                                                        value={clientInfo.birthDate}
                                                        onChange={(e) =&gt; setClientInfo({...clientInfo, birthDate: e.target.value})}
                                                        className=&quot;form-control&quot;
                                                    /&gt;
                                                &lt;/div&gt;
                                                
                                                &lt;div className=&quot;input-group&quot;&gt;
                                                    &lt;label&gt;Адрес&lt;/label&gt;
                                                    &lt;textarea
                                                        value={clientInfo.address}
                                                        onChange={(e) =&gt; setClientInfo({...clientInfo, address: e.target.value})}
                                                        className=&quot;form-control&quot;
                                                        rows=&quot;3&quot;
                                                        placeholder=&quot;Полный адрес проживания&quot;
                                                    /&gt;
                                                &lt;/div&gt;
                                                
                                                &lt;div className=&quot;input-group&quot;&gt;
                                                    &lt;label&gt;Номер страхования&lt;/label&gt;
                                                    &lt;input 
                                                        type=&quot;text&quot;
                                                        value={clientInfo.insuranceNumber}
                                                        onChange={(e) =&gt; setClientInfo({...clientInfo, insuranceNumber: e.target.value})}
                                                        className=&quot;form-control&quot;
                                                        placeholder=&quot;10-значный номер&quot;
                                                        maxLength=&quot;10&quot;
                                                    /&gt;
                                                &lt;/div&gt;
                                            &lt;/div&gt;

                                            {/* Medical Information */}
                                            &lt;div className=&quot;space-y-4&quot;&gt;
                                                &lt;h3 className=&quot;text-lg font-semibold mb-4 text-gray-800&quot;&gt;Медицинская информация&lt;/h3&gt;
                                                
                                                &lt;div className=&quot;input-group&quot;&gt;
                                                    &lt;label&gt;Pflegegrad&lt;/label&gt;
                                                    &lt;select
                                                        value={clientInfo.pflegegrad}
                                                        onChange={(e) =&gt; setClientInfo({...clientInfo, pflegegrad: e.target.value})}
                                                        className=&quot;form-control&quot;
                                                    &gt;
                                                        {Object.entries(pflegegradLevels).map(([key, pg]) =&gt; (
                                                            &lt;option key={key} value={key}&gt;
                                                                {pg.name} - {pg.description[language]}
                                                            &lt;/option&gt;
                                                        ))}
                                                    &lt;/select&gt;
                                                &lt;/div&gt;
                                                
                                                &lt;div className=&quot;input-group&quot;&gt;
                                                    &lt;label&gt;Основной диагноз&lt;/label&gt;
                                                    &lt;select
                                                        value={clientInfo.diagnosis}
                                                        onChange={(e) =&gt; setClientInfo({...clientInfo, diagnosis: e.target.value})}
                                                        className=&quot;form-control&quot;
                                                    &gt;
                                                        {Object.entries(diagnoses).map(([key, diagnosis]) =&gt; (
                                                            &lt;option key={key} value={key}&gt;
                                                                {diagnosis.name[language]}
                                                            &lt;/option&gt;
                                                        ))}
                                                    &lt;/select&gt;
                                                &lt;/div&gt;
                                                
                                                &lt;div className=&quot;input-group&quot;&gt;
                                                    &lt;label&gt;ICF-коды&lt;/label&gt;
                                                    &lt;input 
                                                        type=&quot;text&quot;
                                                        value={clientInfo.icfCodes}
                                                        onChange={(e) =&gt; setClientInfo({...clientInfo, icfCodes: e.target.value})}
                                                        className=&quot;form-control&quot;
                                                        placeholder=&quot;Например: b117.3, d450.2, d920.3&quot;
                                                    /&gt;
                                                &lt;/div&gt;
                                                
                                                &lt;div className=&quot;input-group&quot;&gt;
                                                    &lt;label&gt;Медицинская история&lt;/label&gt;
                                                    &lt;textarea
                                                        value={clientInfo.medicalHistory}
                                                        onChange={(e) =&gt; setClientInfo({...clientInfo, medicalHistory: e.target.value})}
                                                        className=&quot;form-control&quot;
                                                        rows=&quot;4&quot;
                                                        placeholder=&quot;Краткая медицинская история и текущее состояние&quot;
                                                    /&gt;
                                                &lt;/div&gt;
                                            &lt;/div&gt;

                                            {/* Administrative Information */}
                                            &lt;div className=&quot;space-y-4&quot;&gt;
                                                &lt;h3 className=&quot;text-lg font-semibold mb-4 text-gray-800&quot;&gt;Административная информация&lt;/h3&gt;
                                                
                                                &lt;div className=&quot;input-group&quot;&gt;
                                                    &lt;label&gt;Case Manager&lt;/label&gt;
                                                    &lt;input 
                                                        type=&quot;text&quot;
                                                        value={clientInfo.caseManager}
                                                        onChange={(e) =&gt; setClientInfo({...clientInfo, caseManager: e.target.value})}
                                                        className=&quot;form-control&quot;
                                                        placeholder=&quot;Имя куратора дела&quot;
                                                    /&gt;
                                                &lt;/div&gt;
                                                
                                                &lt;div className=&quot;input-group&quot;&gt;
                                                    &lt;label&gt;Источник финансирования&lt;/label&gt;
                                                    &lt;select
                                                        value={clientInfo.fundingSource}
                                                        onChange={(e) =&gt; setClientInfo({...clientInfo, fundingSource: e.target.value})}
                                                        className=&quot;form-control&quot;
                                                    &gt;
                                                        &lt;option value=&quot;kommune&quot;&gt;Kommune&lt;/option&gt;
                                                        &lt;option value=&quot;krankenkasse&quot;&gt;Krankenkasse&lt;/option&gt;
                                                        &lt;option value=&quot;rentenversicherung&quot;&gt;Rentenversicherung&lt;/option&gt;
